2019-01-20 09:43:11,394 [10] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@BinData
SELECT T.BIN_NO
              ,T.CREATION_DATE
              ,CASE T2.BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END BIN_STATUS
              ,CASE T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN '_' THEN '在库' WHEN 'O' THEN '预约出库' WHEN 'I' THEN '预约入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '其他' END BIN_BIZ_STATUS
              ,T.PALLET_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NAME
              ,T1.PRODUCT_GUID
              ,T1.PRODUCT_DATE
              ,T1.PRODUCT_QTY
              ,T1.MAIN_UNIT
         FROM WBS_BIN T
         LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
         LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2 ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1
参数：
@param0=2018/1/19 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/20 0:00:00

2019-01-20 09:43:33,257 [10] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 10:07:15,595 [10] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 10:07:44,861 [10] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC

2019-01-20 10:09:58,900 [10] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

SELECT T.BIN_NO
              ,T.CREATION_DATE
              ,CASE T2.BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END BIN_STATUS
              ,CASE T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN '_' THEN '在库' WHEN 'O' THEN '预约出库' WHEN 'I' THEN '预约入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '其他' END BIN_BIZ_STATUS
              ,T.PALLET_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NAME
              ,T1.PRODUCT_GUID
              ,T1.PRODUCT_DATE
              ,T1.PRODUCT_QTY
              ,T1.MAIN_UNIT
         FROM WBS_BIN T
         LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
         LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2 ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1

2019-01-20 10:12:56,800 [36] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 10:13:54,363 [36] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@SearchBinMaterial
SELECT T1.MATER_NO,
               ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T1.MATER_NO) MATER_NAME,
               SUM(1) BIN_COUNT,
                @param0  as BTIME,
              (1+ @param1 ) as ETIME
          FROM WBS_BIN T
          JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2
            ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
         WHERE T2.USED_FLAG = 1
           AND T2.BIN_STATUS = CHAR(36)
           AND T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = '_'
        AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE >= @param0    AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE <= 1+ @param1    
      GROUP BY T1.MATER_NO, T1.MATER_NAME
      ORDER BY T1.MATER_NO
参数：

@param1=2019/1/20 0:00:00

2019-01-20 10:14:13,108 [36] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 10:14:44,874 [23] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetBillDataTable
select TA.*
        from (SELECT CASE t1.ELOC_NO
           WHEN '00000000' THEN
            '立库'
           ELSE
            t3.loc_name
         END AS ELOC_NAME,
         T1.MATERIAL_NO,t1.product_grade,
          T4.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE AS ORDER_TYPE_MODULE1,
         CASE T4.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE
           WHEN 'I' THEN
            '入库'
           WHEN 'O' THEN
            '出库'
           WHEN 'M' THEN
            '移库'
           WHEN 'T' THEN
            '移载'
         END AS ORDER_TYPE_MODULE,
         T1.ORDER_NO,
         T1.LIMIT_BIN_NO,
         T1.ELOC_NO,
         T1.LIMIT_PALLET_ID,
         T1.LIMIT_PRODUCT_GUID,
         T1.CREATION_DATE,
         T1.DELETE_FLAG,
         T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
         T1.LINE_ID,
         T1.SORT_ID,
         T1.REQUIRE_QTY,
         T1.ACT_QTY,
         T1.SHIP_QTY,
         T1.BIN_ERR_DESC,
         CASE T1.LOCK_END_LOC
           WHEN 0 THEN
            '未锁定'
           ELSE
            '锁定'
         END AS LOCK_END_LOC,
         T1.Line_Status as LINE_NO,
         CASE T1.LINE_STATUS
           WHEN 0 THEN
            '等待'
           WHEN 1 THEN
            '下达'
           WHEN 2 THEN
            '执行'
           WHEN 3 THEN
            '完成'
           ELSE
            '取消'
         END AS LINE_STATUS,
         T1.LINE_STATUS STATUS
          FROM WBS_ORDER_LINE T1
          LEFT JOIN Psb_Material T2
            ON T1.MATERIAL_NO = T2.MATER_NO
          LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T3
            ON T1.ELOC_NO = T3.LOC_NO
          LEFT JOIN WBS_ORDER T4
            ON T4.ORDER_NO = T1.ORDER_NO WHERE T1.DELETE_FLAG='N') TA
       WHERE    TA.STATUS >= 0    
        ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 10:14:45,385 [32] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetTaskDataTable
select TA.*
        from (SELECT T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.EMERGENCY,T.SLOC_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
                CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库' 
                ELSE '移库' END IO_TYPE,
                T.ELOC_NO,T.PALLET_NO,T.PACKAGE_GUID,T.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
                T.SORT_ID,T.CREATION_DATE, T.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,
                CASE WHEN T.TASK_STEP = '0000' THEN '等待' ELSE '执行' END TASK_STEP, 
                T.ROUTE_NOS,T.UNEXE_ROUTE_NO,T.FINISH_DESC,T1.MATER_NO,1 USE_QTY
          FROM WBS_TASK T
          LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        UNION ALL
        SELECT T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.EMERGENCY,T.SLOC_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
                CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库' 
                ELSE '移库' END IO_TYPE,
                T.ELOC_NO,T.PALLET_NO,T.PACKAGE_GUID,T.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
                T.SORT_ID,T.CREATION_DATE, T.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,
                '完成' TASK_STEP, T.ROUTE_NOS,T.UNEXE_ROUTE_NO,T.FINISH_DESC,
                ISNULL(T1.MATER_NO,T2.MATER_NO) MATERIAL_NO,
                1 USE_QTY
          FROM Z50_WBS_TASK T
          LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T2
            ON T2.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID ) TA
       WHERE  TA.ORDER_LINE_GUID = @param0   
      ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE

@param0=Can not Find

2019-01-20 10:14:45,882 [23] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetCmdDataTable
select ta.* from 
          (SELECT T.OBJID,T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.SLOC_PLC_NO,T.ELOC_PLC_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
           WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'M' THEN '移库'
           ELSE '移载' END CMD_TYPE,
           T.PALLET_NO,T.ROUTE_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '10' THEN '堆垛机' WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '20' THEN '输送线' 
           WHEN T.TRANSFER_NO = '30' THEN 'AGV' END TRANSFER_TYPE,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_STEP = '00' THEN '等待' ELSE '下传' END CMD_STEP,
           T.CREATION_DATE,T.EXCUTE_DATE,T.FINISH_DATE, T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID
      FROM WBS_TASK_CMD T
      LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK T1 ON T1.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
      UNION ALL
      SELECT T.OBJID,T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.SLOC_PLC_NO,T.ELOC_PLC_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
           WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'M' THEN '移库' 
           ELSE '移载' END CMD_TYPE,
           T.PALLET_NO,T.ROUTE_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '10' THEN '堆垛机' WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '20' THEN '输送线' 
           WHEN T.TRANSFER_NO = '30' THEN 'AGV' END TRANSFER_TYPE,
           '完成' CMD_STEP,
           T.CREATION_DATE,T.EXCUTE_DATE,T.FINISH_DATE, T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID
      FROM Z50_WBS_TASK_CMD T
      LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK T1 ON T1.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID) ta
       WHERE  TA.ORDER_LINE_GUID = @param0

            '立库'

           WHEN 'T' THEN
            '移载'
         END AS ORDER_TYPE_MODULE,
         T1.ORDER_NO,
         T1.LIMIT_BIN_NO,
         T1.ELOC_NO,
         T1.LIMIT_PALLET_ID,
         T1.LIMIT_PRODUCT_GUID,
         T1.CREATION_DATE,
         T1.DELETE_FLAG,
         T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
         T1.LINE_ID,
         T1.SORT_ID,
         T1.REQUIRE_QTY,
         T1.ACT_QTY,
         T1.SHIP_QTY,
         T1.BIN_ERR_DESC,
         CASE T1.LOCK_END_LOC
           WHEN 0 THEN
            '未锁定'
           ELSE
            '锁定'
         END AS LOCK_END_LOC,
         T1.Line_Status as LINE_NO,
         CASE T1.LINE_STATUS
           WHEN 0 THEN
            '等待'
           WHEN 1 THEN
            '下达'
           WHEN 2 THEN
            '执行'
           WHEN 3 THEN
            '完成'
           ELSE
            '取消'
         END AS LINE_STATUS,
         T1.LINE_STATUS STATUS
          FROM WBS_ORDER_LINE T1
          LEFT JOIN Psb_Material T2
            ON T1.MATERIAL_NO = T2.MATER_NO
          LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T3
            ON T1.ELOC_NO = T3.LOC_NO
          LEFT JOIN WBS_ORDER T4
            ON T4.ORDER_NO = T1.ORDER_NO WHERE T1.DELETE_FLAG='N') TA
       WHERE    TA.STATUS >= 0    
        ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 10:14:50,827 [36] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetTaskDataTable
select TA.*
        from (SELECT T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.EMERGENCY,T.SLOC_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
                CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库' 
                ELSE '移库' END IO_TYPE,
                T.ELOC_NO,T.PALLET_NO,T.PACKAGE_GUID,T.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
                T.SORT_ID,T.CREATION_DATE, T.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,
                CASE WHEN T.TASK_STEP = '0000' THEN '等待' ELSE '执行' END TASK_STEP, 
                T.ROUTE_NOS,T.UNEXE_ROUTE_NO,T.FINISH_DESC,T1.MATER_NO,1 USE_QTY
          FROM WBS_TASK T
          LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        UNION ALL
        SELECT T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.EMERGENCY,T.SLOC_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
                CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库' 
                ELSE '移库' END IO_TYPE,
                T.ELOC_NO,T.PALLET_NO,T.PACKAGE_GUID,T.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
                T.SORT_ID,T.CREATION_DATE, T.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,
                '完成' TASK_STEP, T.ROUTE_NOS,T.UNEXE_ROUTE_NO,T.FINISH_DESC,
                ISNULL(T1.MATER_NO,T2.MATER_NO) MATERIAL_NO,
                1 USE_QTY
          FROM Z50_WBS_TASK T
          LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T2
            ON T2.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID ) TA
       WHERE  TA.ORDER_LINE_GUID = @param0   
      ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE

2019-01-20 10:14:51,360 [29] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetCmdDataTable
select ta.* from 
          (SELECT T.OBJID,T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.SLOC_PLC_NO,T.ELOC_PLC_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
           WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'M' THEN '移库'
           ELSE '移载' END CMD_TYPE,
           T.PALLET_NO,T.ROUTE_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '10' THEN '堆垛机' WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '20' THEN '输送线' 
           WHEN T.TRANSFER_NO = '30' THEN 'AGV' END TRANSFER_TYPE,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_STEP = '00' THEN '等待' ELSE '下传' END CMD_STEP,
           T.CREATION_DATE,T.EXCUTE_DATE,T.FINISH_DATE, T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID
      FROM WBS_TASK_CMD T
      LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK T1 ON T1.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
      UNION ALL
      SELECT T.OBJID,T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.SLOC_PLC_NO,T.ELOC_PLC_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
           WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'M' THEN '移库' 
           ELSE '移载' END CMD_TYPE,
           T.PALLET_NO,T.ROUTE_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '10' THEN '堆垛机' WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '20' THEN '输送线' 
           WHEN T.TRANSFER_NO = '30' THEN 'AGV' END TRANSFER_TYPE,
           '完成' CMD_STEP,
           T.CREATION_DATE,T.EXCUTE_DATE,T.FINISH_DATE, T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID
      FROM Z50_WBS_TASK_CMD T
      LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK T1 ON T1.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID) ta
       WHERE  TA.ORDER_LINE_GUID = @param0   
      ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE

2019-01-20 10:16:46,009 [32] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 10:33:18,872 [32] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 10:36:00,410 [16] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 10:36:20,137 [27] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@SearchBinMaterial
SELECT T1.MATER_NO,
               ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T1.MATER_NO) MATER_NAME,
               SUM(1) BIN_COUNT,
                @param0  as BTIME,
              (1+ @param1 ) as ETIME
          FROM WBS_BIN T
          JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2
            ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
         WHERE T2.USED_FLAG = 1
           AND T2.BIN_STATUS = CHAR(36)
           AND T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = '_'
        AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE >= @param0    AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE <= 1+ @param1    
      GROUP BY T1.MATER_NO, T1.MATER_NAME
      ORDER BY T1.MATER_NO
参数：
@param0=2018/1/19 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/20 0:00:00

2019-01-20 14:18:58,789 [61] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 14:23:59,359 [62] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@SearchBinMaterial
SELECT T1.MATER_NO,
               ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T1.MATER_NO) MATER_NAME,
               SUM(1) BIN_COUNT,
                @param0  as BTIME,
              (1+ @param1 ) as ETIME
          FROM WBS_BIN T
          JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2
            ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
         WHERE T2.USED_FLAG = 1
           AND T2.BIN_STATUS = CHAR(36)
           AND T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = '_'
        AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE >= @param0    AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE <= 1+ @param1    
      GROUP BY T1.MATER_NO, T1.MATER_NAME
      ORDER BY T1.MATER_NO
参数：
@param0=2018/1/19 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/20 0:00:00

2019-01-20 14:24:34,258 [61] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

             '已完成'

             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC

2019-01-20 14:30:58,555 [61] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 14:34:13,010 [78] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 14:37:18,257 [83] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@SearchBinMaterial
SELECT T1.MATER_NO,
               ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T1.MATER_NO) MATER_NAME,
               SUM(1) BIN_COUNT,
                @param0  as BTIME,
              (1+ @param1 ) as ETIME
          FROM WBS_BIN T
          JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2
            ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
         WHERE T2.USED_FLAG = 1
           AND T2.BIN_STATUS = CHAR(36)
           AND T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = '_'
        AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE >= @param0    AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE <= 1+ @param1    
      GROUP BY T1.MATER_NO, T1.MATER_NAME
      ORDER BY T1.MATER_NO
参数：
@param0=2018/1/19 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/20 0:00:00

2019-01-20 14:39:40,198 [61] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 14:40:32,371 [62] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@SearchBinMaterial
SELECT T1.MATER_NO,
               ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T1.MATER_NO) MATER_NAME,
               SUM(1) BIN_COUNT,
                @param0  as BTIME,
              (1+ @param1 ) as ETIME
          FROM WBS_BIN T
          JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2
            ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
         WHERE T2.USED_FLAG = 1
           AND T2.BIN_STATUS = CHAR(36)
           AND T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = '_'
        AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE >= @param0    AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE <= 1+ @param1    
      GROUP BY T1.MATER_NO, T1.MATER_NAME
      ORDER BY T1.MATER_NO

2019-01-20 14:52:17,610 [68] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 15:02:20,613 [11] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

SELECT T1.MATER_NO,
               ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T1.MATER_NO) MATER_NAME,
               SUM(1) BIN_COUNT,
                @param0  as BTIME,
              (1+ @param1 ) as ETIME
          FROM WBS_BIN T
          JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2
            ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
         WHERE T2.USED_FLAG = 1
           AND T2.BIN_STATUS = CHAR(36)
           AND T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = '_'
        AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE >= @param0    AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE <= 1+ @param1    
      GROUP BY T1.MATER_NO, T1.MATER_NAME
      ORDER BY T1.MATER_NO

2019-01-20 15:12:14,935 [10] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

SELECT T1.MATER_NO,
               ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T1.MATER_NO) MATER_NAME,
               SUM(1) BIN_COUNT,
                @param0  as BTIME,
              (1+ @param1 ) as ETIME
          FROM WBS_BIN T
          JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2
            ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
         WHERE T2.USED_FLAG = 1
           AND T2.BIN_STATUS = CHAR(36)
           AND T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = '_'
        AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE >= @param0    AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE <= 1+ @param1    
      GROUP BY T1.MATER_NO, T1.MATER_NAME
      ORDER BY T1.MATER_NO

2019-01-20 15:27:48,120 [44] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN

            WHEN 3 THEN

         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME

    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL

     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'

2019-01-20 15:28:14,198 [44] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@SearchBinMaterial
SELECT T1.MATER_NO,
               ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T1.MATER_NO) MATER_NAME,
               SUM(1) BIN_COUNT,
                @param0  as BTIME,
              (1+ @param1 ) as ETIME
          FROM WBS_BIN T
          JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2
            ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
         WHERE T2.USED_FLAG = 1
           AND T2.BIN_STATUS = CHAR(36)
           AND T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = '_'
        AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE >= @param0    AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE <= 1+ @param1    
      GROUP BY T1.MATER_NO, T1.MATER_NAME
      ORDER BY T1.MATER_NO
参数：
@param0=2018/1/19 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/20 0:00:00

2019-01-20 15:28:54,220 [46] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 15:33:28,410 [35] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetListOutBillLineData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, 
          TL.LIMIT_BIN_NO,
           TL.ELOC_NO,
           TL.LIMIT_PALLET_ID,
           TL.LIMIT_PRODUCT_GUID,
           TL.LIMIT_DATE_START,
           TL.LIMIT_DATE_END,
           TL.DELETE_FLAG,
           TL.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
           TL.LINE_ID,
           TL.SORT_ID,
           TL.MATERIAL_NO,
           TL.REQUIRE_QTY,
           TL.DELETE_FLAG,
           TL.ACT_QTY,
           TL.SHIP_QTY,
           TL.LINE_PRIORITY,
           TL.BIN_ERR_DESC,
           TL.LOCK_END_LOC,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
         WHERE  t1.ORDER_NO =  @param0    
        ORDER BY TL.LINE_ID
参数：
@param0=201901200055

2019-01-20 15:33:36,195 [37] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 16:00:17,010 [8] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@BinData
SELECT T.BIN_NO
              ,T.CREATION_DATE
              ,CASE T2.BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END BIN_STATUS
              ,CASE T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN '_' THEN '在库' WHEN 'O' THEN '预约出库' WHEN 'I' THEN '预约入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '其他' END BIN_BIZ_STATUS
              ,T.PALLET_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NAME
              ,T1.PRODUCT_GUID
              ,T1.PRODUCT_DATE
              ,T1.PRODUCT_QTY
              ,T1.MAIN_UNIT
         FROM WBS_BIN T
         LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
         LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2 ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1
参数：
@param0=2018/1/19 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/20 0:00:00

2019-01-20 16:00:27,840 [41] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 16:00:34,838 [29] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetBillDataTable
select TA.*
        from (SELECT CASE t1.ELOC_NO
           WHEN '00000000' THEN
            '立库'
           ELSE
            t3.loc_name
         END AS ELOC_NAME,
         T1.MATERIAL_NO,t1.product_grade,
          T4.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE AS ORDER_TYPE_MODULE1,
         CASE T4.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE
           WHEN 'I' THEN
            '入库'
           WHEN 'O' THEN
            '出库'
           WHEN 'M' THEN
            '移库'
           WHEN 'T' THEN
            '移载'
         END AS ORDER_TYPE_MODULE,
         T1.ORDER_NO,
         T1.LIMIT_BIN_NO,
         T1.ELOC_NO,
         T1.LIMIT_PALLET_ID,
         T1.LIMIT_PRODUCT_GUID,
         T1.CREATION_DATE,
         T1.DELETE_FLAG,
         T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
         T1.LINE_ID,
         T1.SORT_ID,
         T1.REQUIRE_QTY,
         T1.ACT_QTY,
         T1.SHIP_QTY,
         T1.BIN_ERR_DESC,
         CASE T1.LOCK_END_LOC
           WHEN 0 THEN
            '未锁定'
           ELSE
            '锁定'
         END AS LOCK_END_LOC,
         T1.Line_Status as LINE_NO,
         CASE T1.LINE_STATUS
           WHEN 0 THEN
            '等待'
           WHEN 1 THEN
            '下达'
           WHEN 2 THEN
            '执行'
           WHEN 3 THEN
            '完成'
           ELSE
            '取消'
         END AS LINE_STATUS,
         T1.LINE_STATUS STATUS
          FROM WBS_ORDER_LINE T1
          LEFT JOIN Psb_Material T2
            ON T1.MATERIAL_NO = T2.MATER_NO
          LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T3
            ON T1.ELOC_NO = T3.LOC_NO
          LEFT JOIN WBS_ORDER T4
            ON T4.ORDER_NO = T1.ORDER_NO WHERE T1.DELETE_FLAG='N') TA
       WHERE    TA.STATUS >= 0    
        ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-20 16:00:35,336 [8] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetTaskDataTable
select TA.*
        from (SELECT T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.EMERGENCY,T.SLOC_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
                CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库' 
                ELSE '移库' END IO_TYPE,
                T.ELOC_NO,T.PALLET_NO,T.PACKAGE_GUID,T.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
                T.SORT_ID,T.CREATION_DATE, T.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,
                CASE WHEN T.TASK_STEP = '0000' THEN '等待' ELSE '执行' END TASK_STEP, 
                T.ROUTE_NOS,T.UNEXE_ROUTE_NO,T.FINISH_DESC,T1.MATER_NO,1 USE_QTY
          FROM WBS_TASK T
          LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        UNION ALL
        SELECT T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.EMERGENCY,T.SLOC_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
                CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库' 
                ELSE '移库' END IO_TYPE,
                T.ELOC_NO,T.PALLET_NO,T.PACKAGE_GUID,T.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
                T.SORT_ID,T.CREATION_DATE, T.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,
                '完成' TASK_STEP, T.ROUTE_NOS,T.UNEXE_ROUTE_NO,T.FINISH_DESC,
                ISNULL(T1.MATER_NO,T2.MATER_NO) MATERIAL_NO,
                1 USE_QTY
          FROM Z50_WBS_TASK T
          LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T2
            ON T2.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID ) TA
       WHERE  TA.ORDER_LINE_GUID = @param0   
      ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE
参数：
@param0=Can not Find

2019-01-20 16:00:35,853 [18] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetCmdDataTable
select ta.* from 
          (SELECT T.OBJID,T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.SLOC_PLC_NO,T.ELOC_PLC_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
           WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'M' THEN '移库'
           ELSE '移载' END CMD_TYPE,
           T.PALLET_NO,T.ROUTE_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '10' THEN '堆垛机' WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '20' THEN '输送线' 
           WHEN T.TRANSFER_NO = '30' THEN 'AGV' END TRANSFER_TYPE,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_STEP = '00' THEN '等待' ELSE '下传' END CMD_STEP,
           T.CREATION_DATE,T.EXCUTE_DATE,T.FINISH_DATE, T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID
      FROM WBS_TASK_CMD T
      LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK T1 ON T1.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
      UNION ALL
      SELECT T.OBJID,T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.SLOC_PLC_NO,T.ELOC_PLC_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
           WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'M' THEN '移库' 
           ELSE '移载' END CMD_TYPE,
           T.PALLET_NO,T.ROUTE_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '10' THEN '堆垛机' WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '20' THEN '输送线' 
           WHEN T.TRANSFER_NO = '30' THEN 'AGV' END TRANSFER_TYPE,
           '完成' CMD_STEP,
           T.CREATION_DATE,T.EXCUTE_DATE,T.FINISH_DATE, T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID
      FROM Z50_WBS_TASK_CMD T
      LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK T1 ON T1.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID) ta
       WHERE  TA.ORDER_LINE_GUID = @param0   
      ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE

2019-01-20 16:07:45,832 [29] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService.GetProductStatistics
 
        SELECT TA.*,CONVERT(VARCHAR,ROUND(TA.FG_BIN/TA.TOTAL_BIN,2)*100)+'%' AS USE_RATE,
        CONVERT(VARCHAR,(1-ROUND(TA.DISA_BIN/TA.TOTAL_BIN,2))*100)+'%' AS STO_RATE FROM (
        SELECT * FROM (SELECT TOP 99.9999 PERCENT CONVERT(VARCHAR, T.Real_Group_No) AS ROW_NO,
        COUNT(CASE T.BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) AS FG_BIN,	-------------物料
        COUNT(CASE T.BIN_STATUS WHEN  '_' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) AS EMPTY_BIN,   -------------空库位
        COUNT(CASE T.USED_FLAG WHEN 0 THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) AS DISA_BIN,		-------------禁用库位
        (COUNT(CASE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'P' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END)
        + COUNT(CASE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'E' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END))
        AS ERR_BIN,																-------------异常库位(空出库位，先入库位)
        (COUNT(CASE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'I' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END)
        + COUNT(CASE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'O' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END))
        AS RES_BIN,																-------------预约库位
        COUNT(*) AS TOTAL_BIN,
		T.Real_Group_No
        FROM PSB_BIN_STATUS T
        GROUP BY  T.Real_Group_No
		ORDER BY T.Real_Group_No) T1								-------------总库位
        UNION  
        SELECT * FROM (SELECT TOP 99.9999 PERCENT '总计' AS ROW_NO,
        COUNT(CASE BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) AS FG_BIN,				-------------物料
        COUNT(CASE BIN_STATUS WHEN '_' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) AS EMPTY_BIN,					-------------空库位
        COUNT(CASE T.USED_FLAG WHEN 0 THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) AS DISA_BIN,					-------------禁用库位
        (  COUNT(CASE BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'P' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END)
        + COUNT(CASE BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'E' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END))
        AS ERR_BIN,																-------------异常库位(空出库位，先入库位)
        (COUNT(CASE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'I' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END)
        + COUNT(CASE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'O' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END))
        AS RES_BIN,																-------------预约库位
        COUNT(*) AS TOTAL_BIN,
		99999999 AS Real_Group_No
        FROM PSB_BIN_STATUS T 
		) T2
		) TA
		ORDER BY  Real_Group_No

2019-01-20 16:57:11,341 [20] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.TaskService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.TaskService.GetCrnForkErrorStatus
 
        SELECT FS.CRN_NO,
              FS.CRN_FORK_NO,
              FS.TASK_NO,
              CASE FS.TASK_TYPE WHEN 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '出库' END AS TASK_TYPE,
                CASE WHEN T2.ERR_NAME IS NULL THEN '正常' ELSE T2.ERR_NAME END AS FAULT_NAME,
              --FS.FROM_BIN,FS.TO_BIN,
			  FS.ACTPOSX,FS.ACTPOSY,
              FS.FIP_FAULT_NO,
              FS.FIP_DATE,
              FS.FIP_HANDLE_RESULT,
              CASE FS.FIP_FLAG WHEN 0 THEN '正常' WHEN 1 THEN '待确认' WHEN 2 THEN '已确认' WHEN 3 THEN '已处理' END AS FIP_FLAG
        FROM PEM_CRN_FORK_STATUS FS 
        LEFT JOIN PSB_CRN_ERR T2 ON FS.FAULTNO = T2.ERR_NO
       ORDER BY FS.CRN_NO,FS.CRN_FORK_NO

2019-01-20 16:58:02,507 [18] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.CrnService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.CrnService.GetCrnDataTable
 
      SELECT T.CRN_FORK_NO,T.CRN_FORK_ENABLE,T1.*,
             CASE T.CRN_FORK_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_FORK_ENABLE_DESC,
             CASE T1.CRN_IN_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_IN_ENABLE_DESC,
             CASE T1.CRN_OUT_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_OUT_ENABLE_DESC
        FROM PSB_CRN_FORK T
        JOIN PSB_CRN T1 
          ON T1.CRN_NO = T.CRN_NO
